Our community, marketing and product teams use the communication center to send timely updates, event invites, training materials, and gather product feedback. Mobilize enables us to scale to new cities, drive more signups and build stronger relationships within our community.”</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</blockquote>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"types-quote__author\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"types-quote__person\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"types-quote__person-photo-wrapper\"><img src=\"/img/home/testemonials/adam-faludi.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"types-quote__person-photo\" width=\"54\" height=\"54\"></p>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"types-quote__person-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"types-quote__person-name\">Adam Faludi</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"types-quote__person-position\">Director of Community Engagement</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"types-quote__company\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<svg class=\"types-quote__company-logo svg-icon\" width=\"100\" height=\"40\"><use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"#icon-logo-scoop--dark\"></use></svg>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"types__description features-collapsible__content\">Engage and retain your workforce. Segment by location or expertise, invite them to training sessions, and notify them about opportunities or changes.</p>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"types__button\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<button class=\"action-button js-open-popup js-analytics\" data-label=\"Ondemand workforce - sign up free\" type=\"button\">Sign Up Free</button>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t</section>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<section class=\"types__section tabs__tab features-collapsible\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<h3 class=\"types__section-title features-collapsible__trigger\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"features-collapsible__icon-wrapper\"><svg class=\"features-collapsible__icon svg-icon\" width=\"31\" height=\"30\"><use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"#icon-home-tenant-network\"></use></svg></span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tCoworking Space\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<svg class=\"features-collapsible__arrow svg-icon\" width=\"11\" height=\"7\"><use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"#icon-features-collapsible-arrow\"></use></svg>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</h3>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"types__description features-collapsible__content\">Keep track of tenants or coworking space members.
